| <span data-ttu-id="e3da1-451">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e3da1-451">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e3da1-452">Value</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e3da1-452">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="e3da1-1598">Observaciones</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e3da1-1598">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e3da1-1599">La clase **MS-DFSR-Subscriber** forma parte de la compatibilidad con el servicio de replicación sistema de archivos distribuido (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e3da1-1599">The **ms-DFSR-Subscriber** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
